Pacific Grand Maneuvers: U.S. Fleet Departs from Los Angeles; Over a Hundred Warships File Out of San Francisco; Flagship Leads the Way, Military Spectacle is Magnificent; Maneuver Area Reaches Five Million Square Miles; Starts This Friday and Continues for Six Weeks 29

This is the First Time the U.S. Navy's Maneuvers Have Crossed International Borders

The Flagship USS Pennsylvania: The U.S. fleet departed from San Pedro Harbor at dawn this morning and will conduct large-scale maneuvers in the North Pacific in great secrecy until it returns to California waters on June 10th. "Question Sixteen" is the basic fleet for this year's annual maneuvers, and this year's spring maneuvers are the largest peacetime exercises in the history of the U.S. Navy. May 3rd is the official start date for the maneuvers, and the waters near Alaska will be the focus. There are also 460 aircraft participating in the maneuvers. (29th Guomin News Agency Dispatch)

San Diego, USA: The U.S. Navy is scheduled to hold grand maneuvers in the Pacific Ocean from May 3rd to June 10th, commanded by Navy Commander-in-Chief Admiral Leffers. A total of 164 warships and 450 aircraft will participate in the maneuvers. The maneuver program is kept secret, but it is expected to be a prolonged defense of the Aleutian Islands, with light fleets responsible for defense and main battleships attacking from the south. The naval fleet participating in the maneuvers is under orders not to sail within 3,200 kilometers of Japan. Finally, the fleet will maneuver in the waters off Honolulu before concluding. (29th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

(San Francisco) The U.S. fleet, consisting of 153 warships of various types, set sail from San Pedro tonight and will conduct six weeks of grand maneuvers in the Pacific Ocean. The ships followed the battleship Pennsylvania in single file, creating a magnificent military spectacle. The fleet is commanded by Admiral Leffers, with the Pennsylvania as the flagship. The maneuver area covers approximately five million square miles, starting from Alaska and ending at Midway Island. The main battleships are sailing towards the Hawaiian Islands, while some ships are heading to Puget Sound and the Aleutian Islands. After the main force arrives in Honolulu, it will be divided into two branches. One will continue to Midway Island to establish a temporary base for maritime aircraft, and the other will remain in Honolulu with about 50,000 personnel. Approximately 500 aircraft will participate in the maneuvers. These maneuvers will determine the U.S. Navy's ability to defend various key points. This is the first time that the U.S. Navy maneuvers have reached international borders. Midway Island, two small islands in the sea between North America and Asia, will be a key point in this strategy. Naval aircraft will use it as a fuel base. The aircraft may even fly near Wake Island, which is located to the southwest. President Luo placed this island under naval administration in his order. If aircraft fly from Midway Island to that location, warships will also follow. If so, it will be less than 500 miles from the Far Eastern territory of Japan, formerly belonging to Germany and now administered by Japan, the Marshall Islands. Midway Island is located between the Marshall Islands and the Hawaiian Islands. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

U.S. Navy Giant Aircraft Testing Combat Power 30

(Washington) The Navy Department is maintaining strict secrecy regarding the testing of giant combat aircraft for first-line defense. One giant aircraft is currently undergoing its final test flight on the West Coast by naval officers to assess its combat effectiveness. Another will soon be test-flown in Norfolk. If the test flight results are satisfactory, the Navy Department may order 30 of these aircraft, costing $150,000 each, and it will take a year to build all of them. These aircraft can carry bombs and machine guns and are truly the most powerful weapons. Naval officials plan to organize a first-line defense air force with 30 of these aircraft to resist naval attacks. The aircraft being tested carries six machine guns and two tons of bombs, and can fly 3,000 miles in one go. According to current plans, after these aircraft are built, they will be distributed to the East and West Coasts, and some will be stationed at Pearl Harbor in Hawaii. These aircraft will certainly increase the United States' power to control the Pacific. Naval officers say that their initial intention was to develop these aircraft for reconnaissance and bombing. These aircraft should be able to fly 3,000 miles in one go. The aircraft being tested on the West Coast was manufactured by the Douglas Aircraft Factory in Santa Monica, California. It has a wingspan of 100 feet, two 830-horsepower engines, and a fuselage that can accommodate eight people. The aircraft has already undergone preliminary testing. The aircraft was transported to the sea at dawn, and the surrounding area was heavily guarded, and onlookers were prohibited from taking photographs. It is said that the Navy Department will decide whether to proceed with its aircraft purchase plan after full testing in six days. All aircraft will not be delivered until the second half of 1936. (28th Guomin News Agency Dispatch)

(Washington) The bill for building six army aviation bases on the coasts of the American Atlantic, Pacific, and Alaska has been approved by the House Army Committee and reviewed by the Army Department. It is now learned that a clause must be added when the bill is finally passed, vaguely stipulating that a strong aviation base be built in the Great Lakes region of the United States bordering Canada. According to Deputy Chief of Staff Coalpoon, who recently declared to the House Army Committee, it is currently impossible to make people believe that it is necessary to fortify the Canadian border, but the Army Department believes that an airfield in the Great Lakes region is beneficial to the protection of border people. (28th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

Another Breach of Contract: Germany Rebuilds Navy; Reportedly Will Formally Notify Signatory Nations 31

Ordering Twelve New Submarines; Possessing Long-Range Offensive Capabilities

(Paris) A London correspondent for the Morning Post claims that British officials expect the German government to deliver a note to the ambassadors of all signatory nations to the Treaty of Versailles in Germany today, announcing its naval shipbuilding program and stating that the German government has decided to immediately build twelve submarines, each with a displacement of 250 tons. (29th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

(Berlin) Although local authorities refuse to comment on the rumor that Germany is violating the Treaty of Versailles and is currently engaged in building several submarines, according to reliable sources, the German government has ordered twelve submarines from the well-known Blohm & Voss shipyard in Hamburg and the shipyards in Kiel and Stettin. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) According to the Daily Express, the cabinet will soon discuss whether to protest to Germany over the construction of twelve submarines in violation of the Treaty of Versailles. The Daily Telegraph's naval reporter, Belwarder, said that the submarines built by Germany are not purely defensive in nature, as the country claims, but actually possess long-range offensive capabilities, and their range of activity actually exceeds the Strait of Gibraltar. He also said that the 250-ton submarines currently being built by Germany may even have greater combat power than the submarines used in the European War. (29th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

Air Force Lags Behind; Great Anxiety Arises in Britain; Cabinet is Studying Innovation Plans 32

(London) According to the diplomatic reporter of the Daily Telegraph, since learning that the British Air Force is far inferior to Germany's, great fear has arisen in British political circles. The cabinet is currently studying various plans to innovate the air force. The newspaper also said that the true meaning of Germany's efforts in aerial development lies in organizing an aircraft industry based on the entire country. The decline of the British aircraft industry is due to the inability to sell military aircraft and civilian long-distance aircraft. It is hoped that the British government will pay special attention to this matter. (29th Guomin News Agency Dispatch)

(London) Germany's recent active rearmament, especially in the air force and navy, is causing considerable fear here, as can be seen from the editorials in this morning's newspapers. The Times stated that the news of Germany building submarines surprised the cabinet. The British cabinet had already received news two weeks ago that Germany had completed the assembly of various submarine parts manufactured last winter according to the plan set last year, and now the government has ordered them to be completed immediately. As Britain and Germany will hold a naval conference at the beginning of next month, it is no wonder that the government is greatly surprised that Germany has suddenly announced the construction of submarines before the naval conference. In short, Hitler has always believed that the military clauses in Part V of the Treaty of Versailles can no longer bind Germany. This announcement of the construction of ships prohibited by the Treaty of Versailles is also to show that Germany is no longer bound by the military clauses of the treaty. The Daily Telegraph stated, "The situation created by Germany's implementation of naval rearmament will not change British foreign policy, but British defense plans must be modified. Because Germany has made this decision regardless of everything, Britain's efforts to seek European security solely through international agreements are insufficient, and it must seek other methods to guarantee peace." The Morning Post stated, "The German Ministry of Defense's denial of building a navy shows Hitler's efforts to seek the sympathy of Britain. Although the British people are indifferent to events on the European continent, they cannot ignore Germany's revival of its navy. This is well known to Hitler. Whether Britain can establish a naval agreement with Germany to replace the naval clauses in the treaty, so that Germany's rearmament of its navy becomes legitimate, must be decided. If Britain's purpose is to establish a naval agreement with Germany, other naval powers that signed the Washington and London naval treaties will inevitably oppose it, especially France; however, in short, if British politicians continue to propose such methods without increasing their own national defense, the British-German talks will not only be useless but also harmful." (29th Havas News Agency Dispatch)

United States Temporarily Remains Silent 33

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull is unwilling to criticize the report from London that Germany's naval construction plans are tearing up the Treaty of Versailles. Hull said today that there is still no "official news," so it would be completely "inappropriate" for the United States to issue an official statement. General observers in the United States believe that this move by Germany has violated the Anglo-German Naval Agreement, so if the United States lodges a protest, it will be based on this. According to the Associated Press, a senior spokesman for the German Navy stated that Germany believes that the clauses in the Treaty of Versailles regarding land, sea, and air forces have long been invalid, so the German government's plan to rebuild the navy is to obtain the final "security." As for the London news, it is said that the Anglo-German naval talks will continue according to the original procedure. Today, according to reliable sources, the French Minister of the Navy will visit London at the beginning of next week. The government has also made an official announcement that the Minister of the Navy's daughter is getting married in London, hence this trip. However, the general public believes that the true purpose of this trip is related to the naval talks. (28th Guomin News Agency Dispatch)

Observations of the Japanese Naval Authorities on the Future of the Naval Conference 34

(Tokyo) The naval disarmament issue has been completely stalled since the breakdown of the preparatory consultation in December last year. Recently, the European political situation has greatly changed. Britain advocates inviting Germany and Russia to participate in the disarmament conference, while the United States hopes to postpone the meeting. The situation is gradually becoming complicated. The Japanese naval authorities attach importance to the future. The various situations regarding the naval disarmament conference recently are generally as follows:

(1) Comparison of naval forces of European countries:

Britain: 1.25 million tons, France: 660,000 tons, Italy: 420,000 tons, Soviet Russia: 210,000 tons, Germany: 110,000 tons.

Although Soviet Russia has more than double the tonnage of Germany, Germany's warships are mostly new, so their forces are equal.

(2) Germany wants to obtain 35% of Britain's naval armament (i.e., 440,000 tons), but Britain intends to oppose it for fear of insufficient strength in the North Sea. However, due to air force and other factors, Britain cannot but recognize Germany's acquisition of 15%.

(3) France is most afraid of Germany's expansion of armaments. If Britain recognizes Germany's possession of more than 200,000 tons, then France will also expand its strength to be able to confront it.

(4) The purpose of Britain's invitation to Germany and Russia to participate in the conference seems to be to break through its predicament. However, its future has a significant relationship with the European political situation and can control the fate of the disarmament conference. (29th Jiji News Agency Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The impact of Germany's rearmament on the upcoming formal disarmament conference is viewed by the Japanese naval authorities as follows: If Britain recognizes Germany's demand for 35% of Britain's 440,000 tons, it will be equal to Britain's strength, so it will definitely reject its demand. This is because Britain has recently gradually shifted from the two-power standard to the three-power standard. That is, if Germany is recognized for 440,000 tons, then the combined 660,000 tons of France and 420,000 tons of Italy will reach 1.52 million tons, which will surpass Britain's possession of 1.25 million tons and fundamentally overturn the three-power standard, so it will definitely not agree to give it 35%. From this point of view, Britain will certainly oppose reducing its current possessions, and the Japanese government's fundamental disarmament policy, which calls for stipulating the maximum common holdings and reducing holdings, will also fall into a position of being unable to comply. France has always advocated maintaining the state of the Washington Treaty in terms of its superiority over Germany. Coupled with the fact that the United States insists on its own views, the next disarmament conference, given the current state of affairs in European countries, has even less hope of success. (29th Dentsu News Agency Dispatch)

Hungary Requests Three Conditions for Joining the Danube Convention 39

Changing the current military system is a prerequisite; the principle of revising the treaty should be maintained; Italy, Austria, and Hungary are scheduled to meet early next month for discussion

(Rome) The governments of Italy, Austria, and Hungary, in accordance with the provisions of the Rome Tripartite Protocol of March 17 last year, will hold a meeting in Venice on May 4. The purpose is to discuss the position to be adopted at the nine-nation Danube Conference. This meeting of the three countries was initiated due to several questions raised by the Hungarian government. Hungary has proposed three demands regarding the Danube Convention:

(1) The principle of revising the treaty should be maintained. Any movement to revise the treaty should not be regarded as a violation of the principle of non-interference in internal affairs.

(2) The rights of minorities should be defined. If minorities submit applications to protect their due rights, these applications should not be regarded as violations of the non-interference in internal affairs agreement.

(3) Hungary's signing of the non-interference in internal affairs agreement should be conditional on changing the current military system as a prerequisite. It is generally believed that the Italian government advocates that, before the opening of the nine-nation Danube Conference, Italy, Austria, and Hungary should first study the above-mentioned proposals by the Hungarian government in order to determine a common position for the three countries. In addition to signing the non-interference in internal affairs agreement, the nine-nation Danube Conference is also expected to have the nine countries mutually sign a bilateral mutual assistance agreement to ensure the implementation of the non-interference in internal affairs agreement. Regarding this, Hungary has indicated that it is feasible for Italy and Austria to sign a mutual assistance agreement, but Hungary intends to sign a relatively easier treaty with other related countries. (Havas dispatch, 28th)

Veteran of the French Diplomatic Circle Recounts Past Events of the European War; The British Emperor Once Sent a Warning to Germany 47

(Paris) Mr. Barrère, a well-known diplomat who previously served as the Director of the Political Department of the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs before the European War and is now retired, recently wrote an article published in the Revue des Deux Mondes. It states that when Campbell saw British Emperor George at Windsor Palace on February 1, 1913, the Emperor told him that Prince Henry of Prussia, the German Emperor's brother, had recently visited England on a diplomatic mission and subtly revealed that Austria and Russia might resort to arms, and Germany was determined to intervene militarily. Prince Henry then asked the Emperor whether Britain would participate. The Emperor replied that he would certainly participate in certain circumstances. Prince Henry was very surprised to hear this, saying that the possibility of a British-German war was something that Berlin never dreamed of. The British Emperor replied that, in order to respect honor, we must remain loyal to our allies. Barrère also said that in 1913, the French Commissioner in Cairo spoke with Lord Kitchener. Kitchener warned the French authorities not to rely on the assistance of the British army, saying that the British army was sharp in fighting black people, but its equipment was not sufficient to cope with a European war. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Mexico and the US Government Discuss Silver Issues in Washington; The Meeting Lasted One Hour, the Content is Secret; The US Treasury Secretary Announces That There Will Be No Change in Silver Prices 48

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated today that there will be no change in the silver price of 77.57 cents before tomorrow. (Reuters dispatch, 28th)

(Washington) Today, senior officials from the United States and Mexican governments discussed the silver situation here for an hour. After the meeting, neither side was willing to announce the content of the talks, but said that another meeting would be held in the future. Representing the Mexican government were Mexican Undersecretary of Finance Lopez and Mexican Ambassador to the United States Roé. Representing the United States were Treasury Secretary Morgenthau, Treasury Undersecretary Oliphant, and State Department Economic Advisor Feis. (Reuters dispatch, 28th)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau recently conferred with Roberto, an aide to the Mexican Treasury Secretary, on the silver issue. Discussions will continue thereafter. It is generally believed that Lopez has made a request to the United States government, saying that the United States' silver purchasing process should proceed slowly. Lopez came here by plane from Mexico, accompanied by Rockhill, the commercial counselor of the US Embassy, after the Mexican government announced the withdrawal of silver coins and the prohibition of silver coin exports, in order to confer with Treasury Secretary Morgenthau on the silver issue. (Havas dispatch, 28th) Mexico officially announced today that the Bank of Mexico will reopen on Monday and will continue to sell drafts without restrictions at a rate of 3.60 pesos per US dollar. (National Telegram, 28th)

(London) The London financial community is extremely concerned about the US silver purchasing policy and the repercussions it has caused. The recent decision of the Mexican government to completely withdraw silver coins circulating in the market and replace them with paper money proves that the US authorities' policy of raising silver prices is extremely dangerous for silver standard countries. The Mexican government is deeply afraid that after the silver price rises, the country's silver coins will flow out of the country, creating a temporary phenomenon of currency contraction. Therefore, it has no choice but to take measures to withdraw silver coins. China is in a position as serious as Mexico's. According to speculation in the London financial community, the Chinese government is now planning to strengthen control over Chinese commercial banks, so that they will store silver and issue paper money. In the future, it also plans to implement nationalization of silver. In short, the serious situation created by the US monetary miscalculation may force the Chinese government to change its banking and currency system, so that it can be centrally managed by the central government. Some people believe that this policy of the Chinese government can achieve the expected results. In the future, China will no longer borrow money from international or Japanese sources, and its finances can be easily managed. As for India, the situation is different. Although the rupee used in India is a silver coin, its price fluctuates with the pound sterling. After the silver price rises, the actual price of the rupee exceeds the face price. Therefore, those who hold rupees will sell the silver coins and buy pound sterling, causing the price of the pound sterling to rise. The British government's policy of suppressing the price of the pound sterling in order to develop foreign trade will be greatly affected as a result. In short, people in the London financial community believe that if this situation continues to develop, it will inevitably affect the monetary economy of most countries and produce serious consequences. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Remarks by US Congressmen

(Washington) Congressman Day, one of the initiators of the silver purchase bill, discussed the current situation today, saying that the current silver policy of the authorities will eventually promote international currency stability. The United States' move to increase the value of domestic mined silver to 77.57 cents is now absorbing the liquid supply of silver in the world. Many countries have almost no gold, while the United States has half of the world's gold. It is difficult to manage a currency that is not based on precious metals well, and all countries in the world know this. Now that the United States has absorbed all the silver it can get, some other countries have to raise silver prices to prevent the outflow of silver. The US silver price will eventually be 1.29 dollars. Such competition is difficult to sustain, because some other countries need silver more urgently than the United States. If they currently allow the United States to purchase their silver, they will inevitably have to purchase silver back from the United States in the future. Therefore, they would rather pay a higher price to prevent the outflow of capital. This is inevitable. In the end, the entire matter will be resolved at the International Monetary Conference, which is what President Roosevelt wants. He personally believes that this conference will definitely reach an agreement to establish a global bimetallic system with a ratio of gold to silver of 16 to 1. Congressman Summers, Chairman of the House Currency Committee, said that the US silver price has increased too sharply, as can be seen from the current situation in Mexico. The silver price should be increased gradually so as not to disrupt the general financial situation too much. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau and his staff are closely monitoring the world's reaction to the US policy and are prepared to continue discussions with Mexican Undersecretary of Finance Lopez. It is believed that the Mexican government will ask the United States to moderate its silver purchase policy. Lopez came here from Mexico in order to personally study everything. He told reporters today that the United States and Mexico have found a way to cooperate on this matter. (Reuters dispatch, 28th)

Criticism from London Newspapers

(London) Today, newspapers here continue to criticize the US silver policy, all saying that the US authorities are embarrassed by the results of their own policy. People in the London financial community refer to this policy as chaotic behavior that does not consider future impacts. According to news from New York, the US silver policy aims to prevent the pound sterling from continuing to fall or to force the world to hold an international monetary conference in order to adopt a bimetallic system. London financial reporters do not believe that the US policy can achieve this goal. Moreover, the United States has not purchased silver on foreign markets in the past half month, so the inside story of the US government's policy is even more dubious. The Morning Post said that if there is a danger of a sharp drop in silver prices, the United States will enter the market for policy reasons and maintain it. The Times said that even if the US Treasury Department decides to reduce or temporarily moderate purchases on foreign markets, silver prices may not fall sharply, because speculators believe that the United States will continue its silver policy. A reaction of taking profits is bound to occur at any time. Permanent changes in the silver market can only occur after the United States completely changes its policy. The reaction of China to the US policy has not yet been heard. How things will turn out is of great concern. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Roosevelt Urges National Cooperation to Promote the Work Relief Plan and Says That the Atmosphere of Recovery is Strong 49

(Washington) In a radio address from the White House, President Roosevelt asked the people of the country to ensure that this unprecedentedly large economic program in the world is truly successful, saying that the work relief responsibility he bears is the same for the American people, without allowing for partisan or political differences. However, it must be acknowledged that such large-scale undertakings, implemented in more than 3,000 towns across the country, may have inefficient management, mismanagement, or abuse of funds, and those who criticize it may use this to claim that the entire plan has failed. It should be known that any major undertaking is bound to have some shortcomings, and no class can guarantee that there will be no faultfinders. The most effective way to eliminate these abuses is for the American people themselves to take serious action. He asked the people of the country to cooperate with him to make this public undertaking, which is rare in the world, a model of efficiency and integrity. The government will do its best to use these funds to relieve unemployment. This is the nation's war to eliminate forced idleness, and it contains no other colors or discrimination. President Roosevelt also stated the legislative program he plans to implement during this congressional session, the main ones being the expansion of the National Recovery Administration, the elimination of non-essential public utility silver companies, the implementation of the new banking bill, and the passage of the economic security program. President Roosevelt elaborated on his idea of extending the work of the Recovery Administration, saying that we must continue to protect children, enforce minimum wage systems, prevent excessive working hours, and protect collective bargaining. President Roosevelt advocated for the speedy passage of improvements to the Federal Reserve System, saying that this system has proven its value in the past 20 years. President Roosevelt concluded by saying that the United States has gone through all kinds of hardships, and now still has the confidence to overcome the future. Panic is gradually decreasing, credit is gradually recovering, and there is now a definite atmosphere of recovery. (Reuters dispatch, 28th)

(New York) Wall Street believes that President Roosevelt's radio address is the president's last force to promote the recovery movement. Japanese Immigration to Eastern Hebei; First Batch of 1,000 People to Immigrate by July; Aiming to Create a Mixed Sino-Japanese-Korean Area 92

Tianjin Correspondence: Japanese immigration to Eastern Hebei is currently being actively pursued. This matter is being handled by the Japanese Special Service Agency in Shanhaiguan and the Japanese Consulate-General in Tianjin, in accordance with the orders of its military headquarters, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. A general immigration headquarters has been established in Shanhaiguan, with branch offices in Tangshan, Changli, Luanxian, Leting, and other places, each carrying out its responsibilities. The general and branch offices have hired the heads of local Japanese and Korean residents' associations, presidents of chambers of commerce, and presidents of veterans' associations to assist in the implementation of all plans. The first batch is scheduled to immigrate 1,000 people this year in July, designated to live along the railway line. Those who engage in industry and commerce will be introduced and guided by the Immigration Department. Three months after the first batch of immigrants, depending on the results and management, the second and third batches will be immigrated. The Japanese Consulate-General in Tianjin, in order to handle this matter, recently sent Consul An to inspect various places in Eastern Hebei. The Japanese consulates and police branches in Changli, Tangshan, Shanhaiguan, and Qinhuangdao, and the Japanese police branches in Leting, Miyun, and other places, have all increased personnel a week ago to carry out work, investigate the economy and commerce, and plan residential areas. For a time, the work was quite tense. Among the first batch of immigrants, it has been decided that 600 will be Japanese, mostly residents of Kyushu and Shikoku Islands, and 400 will be Koreans, from poor households in Hamgyong North and South Provinces and Gangwon Province. The purpose is to make Eastern Hebei an area of mixed Sino-Japanese-Korean residence in an invisible way. In reality, they want to make the area along the Beining Railway a continuation of the South Manchuria and Anfeng appendages, and connect it with the puppet state of Manchuria. In Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao, we have no international organizations, and Japanese and Korean people come and go freely. Although Changli, Tangshan, and other places are not treaty ports, the Japanese have set up consulates and police stations. Local officials are afraid of trouble and allow them to carry out their wishes at will. Therefore, there is no way to stop this Japanese immigration to Eastern Hebei this time. This year, Japanese and Korean people have been entering Shanhaiguan, Qinhuangdao, Changli, Leting, Tangshan, and Tanggu in succession, and the number is uncountable. Even in Lulong, Zunhua, Yutian, Fengrun, Qian'an, and Jixian, which are the hinterland of the war zone, the number of Japanese and Korean households and population has also increased since the beginning of spring. Committing crimes and violating the law often makes it difficult for the security authorities to handle. If the Japanese implement their immigration plan within the war zone in July of this year, I do not know what it will be like. (27th)

Harbin; Rapid Development of Japanese Businesses 93

Since the Illegal Transfer of the East China Railway; Japanese Population Soars to 30,000; Bankruptcies of Chinese Businesses Increase Proportionally

Harbin Correspondence: Since the illegal transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the number of Japanese people in Harbin has greatly increased. At the end of last year, there were only 16,000 people, but now it has increased to 30,000. Due to the sharp increase in the Japanese population in Harbin, the business of Japanese stores has also become more prosperous. Therefore, the development of Japanese commerce in Harbin is quite astonishing. The turnover of small merchants has increased by about three times compared to the same period last year. This is due to the rapid development of Japanese commerce after the illegal transfer of the East China Railway. However, on the reverse side, Chinese commercial firms are gradually falling into distress, and have become increasingly depressed. In recent months, there has been an endless stream of closures and bankruptcies. Moreover, due to the increase in railway freight rates by the puppet organization, oil mills, water mills, and lumber merchants are all on the verge of bankruptcy. Further, the increase in the business tax by the puppet organization has caused many capitalists with large sums of money to withdraw their funds. Wealthy merchants from Shandong, Henan, Shanxi, and other places in Harbin have mostly closed their businesses and transferred their capital to the interior. Therefore, the puppet organization has also strictly restricted the remittance of funds by wealthy merchants. These merchants really cannot bear the trampling of the Japanese puppets, and mostly wish to get rid of the harsh rule and return to their hometowns. However, the Japanese in Harbin have an unusually strong sense of patriotism. They all shop at Japanese stores and, except when unavoidable, never trade with Chinese merchants. The crisis of the complete annihilation of Chinese merchants in Harbin and the rapid development of Japanese commerce are directly and inversely proportional. The lifeline of our Chinese commerce will be seized and exhausted by the Japanese. (Northeast Press)

Fujian Province; Relief for Industry and Commerce; Chamber of Commerce Organizes Relief Financial Committee 94

Fuzhou Correspondence: The commercial market in Fujian was previously affected by money houses recalling bills and stopping loans, resulting in a severe stagnation of funds. Therefore, the county chamber of commerce, banking groups, and the provincial government jointly discussed relief methods. It was agreed that the banking groups would release 1 million yuan in loans, and the chamber of commerce would organize a relief financial committee to accept loans from the banking groups and pass them on to reputable money houses for lending to the industrial and commercial sectors to facilitate turnover. Currently, the relief financial committee has been organized, with Luo Mianhou, Song Jingyan, Hong Fasui, Qiu Yisheng, Wan Jianru, Huang Rutaotao, and Liu Aiqi as members. Henghe and Commercial have also been designated as the two money houses for issuing loans, and 400,000 yuan from the Central Bank, 400,000 yuan from the Bank of China, and 200,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications have been allocated and submitted to the head office for approval. However, many days have passed and no approval from the head office has been received, so the funds cannot be released. At this time of year, the tea and timber industries are just beginning to harvest and transport, and industrial and commercial manufacturers are hoping for early implementation to facilitate market circulation. Yesterday, the county chamber of commerce again asked the provincial government to send a quick telegram to Finance Minister Kong to expedite the previous proposal and avoid prolonged waiting. The results of rural loans are still good. In the 23rd year, 100,000 yuan was allocated from the provincial treasury and 100,000 yuan was loaned by the Agricultural Bank of China. Currently, rural loans for the 24th year have begun to be processed, but the provincial treasury is short of funds and has no funds to allocate. Huo Er, Director of the Rural Financial Relief Office, went to Hankou to discuss with the general office of the Farmers' Bank and agreed to re-loan 300,000 yuan to the Rural Relief Office. According to the severity of the disaster in each county, they will be distributed based on the degree of urgency. Each county can receive more than 10,000 yuan or as little as several thousand yuan. Staff will be sent to the border counties in northwestern Fujian within days to guide farmers and organize mutual aid societies as borrowing institutions. Regarding the tea and timber production, which are most closely related to the province's economy, both have declined in recent years. Tea has decreased from 300,000 boxes to 200,000 boxes in the past three years, and pine timber has decreased from 12,000 linked units to over 7,000 in the past three years. The difference in amount is about one-third. Tea and timber merchants bear too heavy a tax burden, which is one of the reasons why trade cannot develop. A special request was submitted to the Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, requesting that the provincial government be consulted on whether to reduce or exempt the special business tax on the tea industry and the temporary defense donation for timber rafts to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. The provincial government has approved a reduction of 30% of the timber raft defense donation, and the tea business tax is difficult to reduce temporarily until compensation can be arranged. Regarding the timber industry, sales of Fujian timber have been excellent recently due to very little timber from North China and the Northeast being transported into the interior, and prices have also risen slightly, which can provide some relief. As for the tea industry, since 50,000 boxes have been transported from northern and eastern Fujian to the province since the beginning of spring, domestic and foreign sales are sluggish, and most of them are piled up in warehouses in the Panfu area on the south bank of the Min River, the future is very pessimistic. (27th)

Troops Stationed in Chaozhou and Meixian Cooperate to Suppress Scattered Bandits on the Fujian Border 95

Shantou Correspondence: Li Mo'an, the pacification commander of the Second District of western Fujian, mobilized six regiments of elite troops to search for remnants of bandits in various counties in western Fujian. Wherever the army arrived, the remnant bandits were defeated at the mere sight of them. Zhang Dingcheng, the bandit leader, led the pseudo-Eighth and Ninth Regiments, as well as independent battalions and guerrillas, to flee to the Xianghu Mountains in Heping County on the Guangdong border, occasionally harassing Dachang and Xiaochang in Dapu County. Chen Shaowu's regiment, which was stationed in Dapu County, sent troops to guard Huliaozhangxi and other places. Now, the bandits are entrenched in Xiaobian, not far from Dachang, and there is a tendency to advance and disturb the Han River. The village chiefs of Dachang have jointly telegraphed the military commanders stationed in the area to send troops to be stationed there to pacify the area. Miao Peinan, the Chief of Staff of the First Army Group, took leave in mid-month to return to his hometown of Wuhua to visit relatives. He took the opportunity to go to Meixian to discuss with Huang Renhuan the method of suppressing the Min bandits, and will be able to go to Chao'an within days to discuss with Deng Longguang's division commander the military secrets of preventing and suppressing the Min bandits. Each army has been preparing to dispatch troops. The bandit nest in Baishui Lake, Phoenix Mountain, Raoping, was attacked by Zhang Guangquan's battalion stationed in Pengxi on the 15th, killing bandits. Knowing that they could no longer stay in Baishui Lake, more than 200 bandits fled to Zhao'an, Fujian, on the evening of the 18th. Currently, many remnant bandits from western Fujian have sneaked into the territory of Chaozhou, mostly gathering in Nanshan, Sangpu Mountain, and Beishan, and have secretly set up institutions in various cities, hoping to cause riots and disturbances. Li Peihua, the captain of the Chao'an County military team, discovered that the Chifen had secretly set up a pseudo-Chao-Cheng-Jie Revolutionary Committee in Dazhai Township, Seventh District. On the morning of the 22nd, he sent a team to encircle and search. When the bandit party saw that things were revealed, they threw bombs to resist arrest. After a fierce battle lasting three hours, the bandit organization was extinguished, and two female bandits, Cai Qiaoxiang and Chen Xixiang, and one male bandit, Liao Yijiao, were captured. Chen Atu, the pseudo-county committee member, was killed. A pseudo-revolutionary committee seal, Mauser pistols, bombs, and many reactionary propaganda items were seized from the bandit's nest. It is heard that bandits have secretly set up institutions in various counties. The Shantou Public Security Bureau conducts a household registration check once a month, and has now temporarily commissioned detective officials as special household registration inspectors. All households in various streets and alleys, if they are suspected households, can be inspected at any time, so that bandits have no way to stay. In order to suppress the remnants of bandits in various counties, long-distance telephones in various counties in the eastern district are limited to be erected and completed by the end of this month. The Meizhou telephone network is connected to Xingning, the Huizhou telephone network is connected to Heyuan, and the Chaozhou telephone network is connected to Chao'an. The General Headquarters sent technician Cai Dongpei to set up a general exchange in three places, and connect them to each other at the same time. Once a bandit police alarm or a Chifen action occurs, troops can be sent to block and intercept them at any time. It is necessary to search out all the remnant bandits in various counties within a short period of time.

Wuxi: Branch Director Fan Dismissed and Investigated 96

Fan Lei (Xin Zhi), Director of the Fourth Public Security Branch, was accused by people in Xili in November of this year for failing to issue tickets for gambling cases. After receiving the order from the Civil Affairs Department to investigate, County Chief Yan immediately dispatched personnel to investigate and truthfully reported the case. Yesterday, the province ordered the county government to the effect that the branch director had detained the district secretary on suspicion of abusing his public office for private purposes, and that the presentation of criminal cases had been delayed for many days without reason, which was especially inappropriate. He was ordered to be dismissed first, and the vacant position was ordered to be filled by the bureau in accordance with the regulations. As for the fact that he privately collected gambling fines and did not issue tickets, it is not without real suspicion, and the case was sent to the court for investigation and legal action.

Gang of Thieves Robs Farmhouse in the Middle of the Night 97

Zhang Jinfu, a villager from Zhangqiaotou in the third district of the county, made a good living by rowing boats, so he was coveted by bandits. At 2:00 AM the other night, more than forty bandits suddenly came, armed with guns, iron bars, and other weapons. They climbed over the wall and entered the bedroom, where they tied up Jin's wife, Shen, on the bed with ropes, forcing her to reveal the hiding place of the silver and forbidding her to make any noise. Then they rummaged through the boxes and arbitrarily searched, and after getting their loot, they opened the door and left with a roar. It is estimated that they were robbed of gold and silver jewelry, cash, clothes, etc., worth about 300 yuan.

Changshu: Villagers in Beigou Township Capture Seven Bandits 98

The other night (the 26th), Wang's house in Zoujiawan, Beigou Township, was suddenly robbed by bandits. The bandits numbered about ten, mostly armed with sharp blades and other weapons, but no guns. After entering the house, the bandits used various vicious means to coerce the victims, but they were detected. The bandits had no guns, so the crowd was immediately gathered and surrounded the bandits, capturing seven bandits on the spot. The Gangkou Public Security Bureau was informed and sent police to take them back for questioning. They confessed to their names: Xu Baokang, Shao Zhongyuan, Chen Fengxiang, Wang Fuxiang, Wang Manquan, Cai Baozhong, Xie Yongbao, and confessed to robbing Xu's house in Daba Township on January 30th of this year, Zhang Qijing's house in He Zhang on February 1st, Song Chushi's house in Langang Bridge on February 12th, Liu Ji's house in Anzhuang Township on February 25th, the Li Taitang Temple in Langshi Bridge on March 17th, Xie Qi Ding Fuyun's house on April 1st, Xu Kanglin's house and Miao Xiaodi's house in Rangtang Township on April 15th, and Zhang Qi Guan's house in Zhang Qi Township on April 18th. The branch bureau has sent all the criminals to the bureau for transfer to the judiciary. They were brought in for questioning at 3:00 PM, and all the criminals confessed as above. They were ordered to be detained.

Nantong: Dasheng Labor Strike Expected to Be Resolved 99

The Dasheng Yarn Factory in Tangjiazha, Nantong, was in financial difficulty and decided to suspend work for several days each month. The workers misunderstood and a strike occurred. Ren Zufeng, a representative of the provincial government and a director with government shares, came to Tong and consulted with Manager Li Shengbo and the directors and supervisors, persuading the workers to be aware, and it is expected to resume work in two or three days.

Jiaxing: Verdict in Agricultural Bank Embezzlement Case 100

The Jiaxing Farmers Bank discovered embezzlement in August of last year. Former manager Wu Heshu even fled in fear of punishment. Subsequently, the main staff members, Tu Yiran and Xu Shu, were sent to the court for investigation. The criminal part has long been decided by the Criminal Court. The civil part was submitted to the court by the current manager, Chen Ruixuan. After summoning the defendants and their guarantors for separate trials, the verdict was announced on the 29th. Wu Heshu, Tu Yiran, and Xu Shu should jointly and severally compensate the plaintiff 35,861.46 yuan, and interest calculated at 5% per annum in accordance with laws and regulations from August 14, 23rd year of the Republic of China until the end of execution. If they are unable to pay, Chu Fucheng, Yang Yaoge, and Song Jinglian shall be jointly and severally liable for the compensation. The plaintiff's remaining claims were rejected. The plaintiff shall bear one-third of the litigation costs, and the defendants Wu Heshu, Tu Yiran, Xu Shu, Chu Fucheng, Yang Yaoge, and Song Jinglian shall jointly and severally bear two-thirds.

Hangzhou: Court Executes Three Sheng Bandits 101

The Zhejiang High Court ruled that the Sheng bandits Sun Lanjin, Zhou Rongting, and Zhang Ating had committed serious crimes of banding together, kidnapping people for ransom, murder, and arson in their hometown of Sheng County. They were wanted. The bandits have been successively captured and sent to Hangzhou. After the court's investigation, the facts were confirmed and they were sentenced to death. The provincial government approved the sentences. Yesterday (29th) at 9:00 AM, the three bandits were taken out, their identities were verified, and they were escorted to the execution ground outside Qingtai Gate and executed by firing squad.

Mingguang: Unprecedented Salt Famine Occurs in Mingguang 102

This port is the salt sales center market for counties such as Jiading. The monthly sales are no less than several thousand piculs. Recently, due to the lack of vehicles, salt transportation has been slow, resulting in the sale of all salt in stock and an unprecedented salt famine. For the past month, salt prices have soared from eleven jin per yuan to five and a half jin. According to recent investigations, only a few dozen bags remain in retail stores throughout the city. Purchases are now limited to half a jin per person. If no more salt arrives within days, there is a danger of having to eat tasteless food.

International Business Telegram

April 29th, Reuters Special Business Report 103

Gold and Silver

London gold prices today (29th) fell by 10.5 pence due to the high exchange rate of the pound, to 144 shillings and 5.5 pence.

The London silver market was very volatile this morning. At closing, the spot price was 34.0625 pence and the futures price was 34.1875 pence, both down 1.0625 pence. Speculators were both buying and selling.

Mount Lyell silver opened today with futures falling by 180 to 200 pounds, but trading was light. It then fell another 50 pounds.

Exchange Rates

The British-American London foreign exchange market was stable today. The British pound had an upward trend. The British-American exchange rate opened at $4.8325, higher by .125 than the US-UK closing rate on Saturday, and higher by 1.25 cents than the previous British-American price. At 11:00 it fell by .0625, then the price gradually rose. At 2:00 PM, the price was $4.833125, up .375 from the opening. Also, one US dollar equaled 4 shillings and 1.657 pence.

The British-French exchange rate opened at 73 francs and 12 centimes, higher by 21 points than the closing rate on Saturday. At 11:00 it fell by 5 points, after which the price recovered. At 2:00 PM, the price was 73 francs and 12 centimes, the same as the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

The New York cotton market opened today (29th) down 6 points. Within the first hour, it fell by 11 points. There was no significant trading activity. The decline in foreign cotton markets caused long positions here to be closed, thus affecting the market situation.

Chicago wheat saw rain in the drylands, and prices fell slightly, but the opening decline was not severe. Trading was limited, and the market was unexciting.

Liverpool wheat: Reports of rain in American wheat regions caused selling in the Liverpool wheat market today. At 1:00 PM, the July futures price was 5 shillings and 6.75 pence, down 1.125 pence from the Saturday closing.

Liverpool cotton also fell today. At 1:00 PM, the July futures price was 6.46, down 9 points.

Rubber

The London market was quiet today with subdued trading. Prices fell slightly. At noon, the July/September futures price was 5.8125 pence, down .0625 from the Saturday closing.

New York opened today down 10 points, mainly due to the brewing labor unrest.

Securities

The New York market opened in disarray this morning, with uncertain sentiment. President Roosevelt's broadcast address regarding legislation to manage public utility companies and abolish public utility holding companies failed to improve sentiment. Public utility stocks, therefore, opened lower and showed weakness. Industrial stocks saw some buying due to positive prospects, but the current uncertainty ultimately hampered the rise. However, the declines were insignificant. Silver mining stocks were the most active, but with the sharp drop in silver prices, sentiment was not very positive. Although some viewed President Roosevelt's broadcast address last night as favorable to long positions, the uncertainty in the silver market had a greater impact. Local News

The "Four Bottoms" Deadline Today, Industry and Commerce Can Hopefully Weather the Storm 104

Interbank Lending Indirectly Aids Industry and Commerce; Money Shops Permitted to Extend Loans with Increased Interest; National Products Groups and City Federation Representatives Petition

Today is the final day for the long-term loans related to the "Four Bottoms" deadline for the industrial and commercial sectors. Due to the major banks such as the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications providing interbank lending for assistance in recent days, and with the industrial and commercial sectors and money shops having made proper prior arrangements, extensions with increased interest have been granted. Therefore, yesterday's situation was very peaceful. Apart from the foreign interbank rate rising from 15% to 18%, there were no other unsettling conditions. Thus, according to sources in the banking and money shop sectors, this "Four Bottoms" deadline can hopefully be weathered safely.

Interbank Lending Reaches Eight Million

The Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and other banks, in assisting with the "Four Bottoms" difficulty, have implemented interbank lending. Since the 23rd of this month, including old loans extended, the total has reached around eight million yuan. After adjustments by the three banks, the market has largely stabilized. Yesterday, on the eve of the "Four Bottoms" deadline, although there were several firms in this city requesting mortgage-backed lending, the amount was small, only two to three hundred thousand yuan. Other banks also made some sporadic small loans. According to sources at the Bank of Communications, the loan distribution method for the joint interbank lending by the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, etc., was originally based on a 4-4-2 system. This year's lending has been changed to a 3-3-3 system, meaning that the Bank of China, Central Bank, and Bank of Communications share the responsibility equally. (Shen Shi News Agency)

Bankers Association Urges Discussion of Measures

The Shanghai Bankers Association, based on the resolution of the 66th Executive Committee meeting on the 27th, sent a letter to the Central Bank yesterday, outlining the progress of handling small industrial and commercial credit loans and the amount raised. A subcommittee has been formed, hoping that the Central Bank will set a date to convene a meeting. The Bankers Association's subcommittee will nominate committee members Ye Fuxiao (Continental Bank) and Wang Yansong (Silk Industry Bank) to attend and participate in the discussions, so as to jointly discuss the organizational methods for the loan syndicate. (Guo Wen News Agency)

National Products Groups Petition for Implementation

The China National Products Maintenance Association, the Mechanized National Products Factories Association, the Shanghai National Products Factories Association, and the Shanghai Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products, etc., formed the National Products Grand Alliance Committee, and representative Gu Xiyuan went to the Central Bank at 11:00 AM yesterday to meet with Governor Kong Xiangxi. Secretary Tan Chonghuan met him on Kong's behalf. Gu requested that the 20 million yuan loan from the three banks to aid industry and commerce be implemented quickly. Tan replied that because the loan needed to be handled jointly with the Bankers Association, the procedures were slightly complicated. The three banks have made considerable preparations, and once they have discussed with the Bankers Association, it should be possible to realize. (Xin Sheng News Agency)

City Federation Representatives Visit Kong and Song Separately

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation held its sixth executive committee meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday. Attendees included Hu Fengxiang, Shen Tianxin, Zhang Xianfang, Zhang Yichen, and Chen Jicheng. Shen Tianxin chaired, and Zhao Ziyun recorded. After the reports were given, they discussed the Ministry of Finance's order for the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank to jointly establish a mortgage-backed loan of 15 million yuan and a credit loan of 5 million yuan. They resolved to urge the quick implementation of these measures to alleviate the people's difficulties and appointed four committee members, Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, Shen Tianxin, and Zhang Xianfang, to separately visit Finance Minister Kong, Bank of China Chairman Song, and Bankers Association Chairman Chen to request immediate implementation.

Money Shops from Ningbo and Zhenhai Come to Settle Accounts

No fewer than seventy or eighty money shops in the Ningbo and Zhenhai areas have dealings with the money shops and industrial and commercial sectors of this city, with the Ningbo group being the most numerous. Every time the "Four Bottoms" and "Ten Bottoms" long-term settlement periods arrive, a large number of money shop representatives come to Shanghai to settle accounts. These representatives have now arrived in Shanghai from Ningbo and Zhenhai one after another. However, some are extending loans, while others are collecting debts, and not all are acting in unison. The actions of these money shop customers are also not carried out in groups, but rather individually or in small groups of two or three.

Increased Demand Causes Foreign Interbank Rate to Rise

The foreign interbank rate in the money market is gradually rising due to the "Four Bottoms" deadline. For example, it was 10% on the 25th of this month, 12% on the 26th, 15% on the 27th and 28th, and 18% yesterday (29th) both in the morning and afternoon. According to the money shop sector, this is a matter of supply and demand and is not a special phenomenon. Once the "Four Bottoms" deadline has passed, it should return to normal. In the future, when silk and tea are on the market and demand is even greater, a surprising peak in the foreign interbank rate will inevitably appear. (Above from Guo Wen News Agency)

Following the continued rise in American silver prices, the Shanghai foreign exchange market has uniformly extended lending. Yesterday morning, the Central Bank announced today's (29th) telegraphic transfer selling prices as follows: London, one yuan in national currency equals one shilling and eight and a half pence; New York, one hundred yuan in national currency equals forty-one US dollars and twenty-five cents; Paris, one hundred yuan in national currency equals six hundred and twenty-two francs; Berlin, one hundred yuan in national currency equals one hundred and one and a half marks. As for the balancing tax rate announced by the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee at 16:00 yesterday morning, it was calculated at 2 shillings and 1.125 pence, which is 6.75%, the same as in recent days. (Xin Sheng News Agency)

Ministry of Finance: Bans Money Shops from Halting Operations Under False Pretenses; Shareholders and Managers Should Be Held Responsible for Clearing Debts; Instructs the Money Shop Association to Investigate Halting Shops in Detail 106

The Ministry of Finance issued an instruction to the Shanghai Money Shop Association yesterday, stating: "Since recent years, whenever there has been an emergency in the market, the Ministry has sent letters to the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank to provide substantial loans to facilitate adjustments. Money shops, having received this assistance, should have developed their operations. However, recently there have still been cases of money shops going bankrupt or ceasing operations for liquidation. Upon closer inspection, the bankrupt and closed shops are not necessarily purely due to bad debts. There are often unscrupulous managers who abuse and embezzle funds or engage in corruption and fraud, using bankruptcy and closure as a means of concealing their crimes. Outsiders, unaware of the truth, often take the closure of money shops as a sign of financial distress, thereby shaking public confidence and affecting the market, which is deeply regrettable. The organizational structure of money shops is generally an unlimited company or partnership. Each shareholder or partner should bear unlimited liability for repayment. Managers and executives should also be held accountable. Money shops that go bankrupt or cease operations cannot evade responsibility until all debts are fully repaid by the managers and executives, along with the shareholders or partners, by simply entrusting a liquidator. Managers and executives who embezzle funds or engage in corruption and fraud should be severely punished according to the law and cannot be excused. Therefore, the association is instructed to promptly and thoroughly investigate the money shops that have recently gone bankrupt or ceased operations. If any of the above circumstances are found, the Ministry should be promptly informed with accurate facts so that legal action can be taken. All colleagues should be informed and must rectify their operations and not halt operations rashly, lest they cause disturbances. This is of utmost importance. This order."

Shanghai Literacy Education Committee: Literacy Movement Week Opens Tomorrow; District Office Directors and Service Team Leaders Take Office Simultaneously; Mayor Wu and Director Pan Serve as Chief and Deputy Chief Leaders; Registration for Literacy School Teachers Begins Tomorrow 107

The Shanghai Literacy Education Committee, in order to expand the publicity for the literacy movement, has designated May 1st as the start of the Shanghai Literacy Education Promotion Movement Publicity Week. The opening ceremony will be held tomorrow at 9:00 AM at the committee's office in the Zhengzhong Primary School on Zhengzhong Road in the city center. At the same time, the directors of the district offices and the leaders of the literacy education service teams will also hold joint inauguration ceremonies. The Shanghai News reporter's notes on the situation are recorded as follows:

Expanded Publicity Opens Tomorrow

The Literacy Movement Publicity Week is scheduled to open tomorrow morning. The first day coincides with Labor Day on May 1st and is designated as Workers' Publicity Day. The General Labor Union will expand its publicity, and major and minor newspapers will write articles on literacy education. All cinemas will show literacy education slides for seven days. May 2nd is Broadcast Day, and the Sino-Western Radio Station will broadcast literacy education programs throughout the day, while all radio stations will simultaneously rebroadcast. May 3rd is Business Publicity Day. The City Chamber of Commerce will issue a letter to merchants on the literacy movement, and literacy slogans will be posted at the entrances of all shops. May 4th is Entertainment Publicity Day. All entertainment circles in the city will mobilize to promote literacy. The Citizens' Education Hall will also hold a costume lecture. May 5th is Film Publicity Day. The World Grand Theater in Zhabei and the Penglai, Republic, and Fu'an theaters in Nanshi will screen films with literacy education themes, including Star Film Company's "Women's Morality," Art China Film Company's "Golden Age," and Lianhua Film Company's "Bright Blind Man," etc. May 6th is Academic Publicity Day. Schools will hold lectures on the significance of literacy education during their commemorative weeks. Students will organize publicity teams. May 7th is Seventh Day Publicity Day. The Mountain City Farmers' Association will issue a letter to farmers, and the district farmers' associations will conduct simultaneous publicity.

District Offices Established Uniformly

All district offices, except for the Jiangwan and South Shanghai districts, which have already been established as experimental district offices, will be established uniformly on May 1st. The directors of the offices are also scheduled to take office on the same day. The names of the directors of each district are as follows: Yichuan District Tao Guangchuan, Wenmiao District Chen Songchun, (Experimental District) Zhonghua District Jiang Menglin, Gaochang District Yu Xiang, Dianmei District Shen Qu, Shishan District Feng Yixian, Datong District Feng Xiancheng, Fahua District Hu Xingyao, Yangsi District Yang Huaichun, Tangqiao District Yuan Chang, Caojing District Tang Shugui, Gaoqiao District Lao Shude, Gaohang District Qu Xing, Yinhang District Lu Hailan, Jiangwan District Yuan Shi, (Experimental District) Pengpu District You Jisheng, Lixing District Sheng Zhensheng, Zhenru District Chen Zhongfu, Pusong District Xu Gongjian, Wusong District Cheng Kuanzheng, Yangjing District Shen Yu, and Yinxiang District Lu Jingtang.

Service Team Leaders Take Office Simultaneously

The literacy education service team leaders are also scheduled to hold a joint inauguration ceremony on May 1st. Mayor Wu will serve as the chief leader, and Director Pan will serve as the deputy chief leader. There will be 300 branch teams, with the principals of all municipal and private primary and secondary schools in the Chinese area serving as branch team leaders. Each school will be a branch team, with one-quarter of the students in each school serving as team members, bearing the responsibility of teaching people to read. Each deputy member must find at least two illiterate people every two months, teach them to read, and set the teaching time themselves. Team members who teach more than three people to read within a period (two months) and who have passed the examination will be awarded a certificate by the branch team leader. Those who teach more than ten people will be awarded a banner by the general team. Those who do not work effectively will be warned by the branch team leader, or have their team membership revoked, or have their civic score deducted appropriately.

Registration for Literacy School Teachers Begins

The committee is holding an examination for teachers for the literacy schools in each district in order to select qualified teachers. Registration will be held at the committee's office from May 1st to May 6th. Candidates must be graduates of secondary schools or above, or have equivalent qualifications and have served as teachers in primary or secondary schools or popular schools for more than one year, be between the ages of 20 and 40, and be able to speak Mandarin and teach it. The examination items include physical examination, written test, and oral test. The quota is said to be 200 people. After being selected, the committee will provide three weeks of training, and then they will be assigned to literacy schools as teachers, with a monthly salary of 20 to 40 yuan for a term of one year.

Art Exhibition: Preview Day 21; Extended for Five Days at the Request of Various Sectors 108

Yesterday (29th) was the 21st day of the Shanghai preview of the London International Exhibition of Chinese Art. The viewing was closed in the morning as usual, and reopened in the afternoon. The audience was extremely crowded, as the exhibition has been running for three weeks, and the number of viewers has been no less than tens of thousands. Everyone praised the preciousness of the antiquities, and the word spread, so more and more people have come to see them in recent days. The news obtained yesterday is compiled as follows:

Extended for Five Days

The association's display of antiquities and public exhibition was originally scheduled to close today (30th), after which packing and shipping to England would take place. However, people from all walks of life believed that the exhibition of ancient artifacts and artworks from various dynasties in our country, held in Shanghai before going abroad, was for the appreciation and study of Chinese and foreign visitors. Given the size of Shanghai and the large population, this unprecedented exhibition was just when the people were paying attention. Closing it suddenly seemed too short a period. It was appropriate to extend the exhibition time and provide convenience for group visits to make it universal and increase people's understanding of their inherent culture, etc. In recent days, various groups have sent letters and telegrams with these reasons, requesting the association to extend the exhibition period. After several considerations, the association decided to extend the exhibition for five days, from May 1st to May 5th, after which no further extensions will be made. Groups that have sent letters requesting an extension, such as the China Art Education Society and the Hangzhou Youth Association, have been replied to individually, and the Shanghai Education Bureau has been notified that the preferential measures for schools and art academic groups will continue to be effective during the extended period. This is the last opportunity to view the association's display of antiquities, and people in Shanghai should not miss it.

Installation of Electric Fans

The number of people visiting the association's antiquities has been increasing every day. In order to improve public health and air circulation, the association has added electric fans to the exhibition hall. Therefore, the air inside the association venue has been very good lately.

Viewers' Notes

The exhibits at the London art exhibition preview are numerous and exquisite. Visitors truly have the impression of walking along the Shanyin Road, unable to take it all in. However, everyone's psychology is different, and the purpose of the visit is different, so what everyone pays attention to is also different. Even with regard to a certain exhibit, there are many different arguments. Those who study painting and calligraphy mostly stroll around the painting and calligraphy room. Those who study bronze and porcelain mostly linger in the bronze and porcelain room. The rest, those who study woodblock prints, those who are skilled in archaeology, and those who love to play with jade, all explore and study according to their preferences. Everyone has their own opinion, and it is not necessary to be the same in principle, nor is it possible to be the same in practice. Among them, the one that attracts the most attention is Qianlong's actual seat. This seat is rectangular, slightly like a sofa for two people, made of purple sandalwood inlaid with cloisonné, with extremely exquisite carvings and inlays, covered with a yellow dragon brocade cushion. Behind the seat is a screen, also made of purple sandalwood inlaid with cloisonné, with a landscape of mountains and pavilions. In front of the seat is a long sandalwood desk. This kind of table is very ordinary, but what is valuable is that the four sides and legs of the table are fully carved with inscriptions by famous people of the time, Liu Yong and Weng Fanggang, and paintings by Zheng Banqiao, Jin Nong, Jiang Nansha, Tang Tiufen, etc. It is said that this table was regarded as a historical treasure in the Qing Palace because of the above-mentioned famous carvings and because it was used by Qianlong. Later, the emperors of the Qing Dynasty did not easily use it. On the table are jade-handled brushes, brush rests, brush holders, ink beds, and water bowls, all made of mutton-fat jade, as well as jade seals, Duan inkstones, and imperial ink. It is said that these are all items used by Qianlong. The audience pays special attention to this and makes many comments. Some say that such a treasure seat and precious furnishings are truly solemn and brilliant, and one can imagine the dignity and wealth of the emperor. No wonder so many people want to be emperors. Some say that being an emperor is nothing more than this. Life is like acting, and the emperor is just a character on the stage. Still others say that the emperor has to sit on the real seat in a well-behaved and proper manner, with the left historian recording words and the right historian recording events, and everything that is said and done is recorded by someone, which is very restrictive. It is better to be a commoner like us and be free. Finally, a very funny lady said that if the association allowed visitors to sit on the real seat for one minute for one yuan, I would definitely spend one yuan to be a fake emperor for one minute. A female companion interjected and said, wouldn't that make you Wu Zetian? This made everyone laugh. Then the female companion said, Wu Zetian is indeed a heroine, and my words are not an insult. From these various conversations, I can see that everyone's psychology is very inconsistent. This treasure seat exhibition room can be used as a psychological testing room. The portraits of emperors in the painting and calligraphy exhibition room, such as the portrait of Emperor Taizu of Song, the portrait of Emperor Taizong of Song, and the portraits of emperors and empresses of the Yuan Dynasty, easily arouse the interest of the general audience, just like the aforementioned treasure seat. The portrait of Genghis Khan, a hero of the European nations, is even more noticeable to Chinese and foreigners for his heroic posture. Other works, such as the Red Hibiscus and White Goose Painting by Emperor Huizong of Song, the Long Scroll of Autumn Evening at the Pond, and the album pages written by him, Zhong Kui Painting by Emperor Shizu (Emperor Shunzhi) of Qing Dynasty, and Emperor Gaozong of Qing Dynasty (Emperor Qianlong)'s copy of Su Zizhan's book, the long scroll of Huang Zigiu's Dwelling in the Fuchun Mountains, and the Yubo Fishing Boat Painting by Emperor Qianlong, Yuan Guan Daosheng (Zhao Ziang's wife)'s stone bamboo, Ming Xing Cijing (woman)'s painting of Buddha statue, etc., are all viewed by artists from the perspective of art itself, while ordinary viewers pay more attention to them because they are either works of emperors or works of famous ladies, and pay special attention to the identity of the author. They appreciate things beyond appearance. There were many visitors that day (29th), and the order was good, which shows that the national morality has greatly improved, which is very gratifying. In addition to visiting the art, I also got to observe the attitudes and psychology of various types of visitors, which was quite interesting. Although I dare not say that I understand the interesting things in the interesting, I can also be regarded as one who can get a taste of the taste outside the taste. Old Pen Notes.

Zeng Zhongming Discusses Railway Department's Construction of Various Lines 109

Arrangements for the Pinghan and Yuehan Railways; Completion of the Huningyong Railway and Construction of the Sujia Railway

A Central News Agency report states that Zeng Zhongming, Vice Minister of Railways, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing a few days ago to negotiate with the financial community regarding the reorganization of the Railway Department's old debts. A Central News Agency reporter visited him at his private residence yesterday morning and inquired about the Railway Department's construction plans for various lines. Mr. Zeng provided detailed information, which is recorded as follows:

Negotiating the Reorganization of Old Debts

Mr. Zeng stated that his visit to Shanghai was to negotiate with the Shanghai financial community regarding the Railway Department's debts and to raise funds for new railway construction. He will remain in Shanghai for another day or two before returning to Nanjing. As for Gu Mengyu, the Minister of Railways, he has been on sick leave for several months. It is now learned that Mr. Gu's illness has subsided, and he will remain in Beiping for another month before returning south to temporarily reside in Lushan, as Mr. Gu's physical condition is inherently weak.

Remarkable Rise in Railway Stocks Overseas

A large number of railway stocks nationwide have been sold on overseas markets. In recent years, due to the development of various railway operations and improved credit, stock prices have been rising steadily. Currently, stock prices are three to four times, or even five to six times higher compared to three years ago. For example, stocks previously sold for £26 have now risen to £96, and stocks priced at £30 have risen to £101, and so on.

Plans for Reorganizing Two Railways

Mr. Zeng then discussed the plans for reorganizing the Pinghan and Yuehan railways. The reorganization of the Pinghan Railway is already underway. The Railway Department, considering the age of the Yellow River Railway Bridge, has consulted with railway experts and the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission to study solutions. They have determined that the river surface at that location is wider and the geological conditions are looser, making it necessary to select a new site for construction. The estimated cost is between 20 and 30 million yuan. As for the Yuehan Railway, construction is currently underway in sections and is expected to be open to traffic around December next year.

Completing the Huningyong Railway

The completion of the Huningyong Railway is also actively underway. The Qiantang River Railway Bridge is under construction by the Railway Department and the Zhejiang Construction Department and is expected to be completed next year. The second step will be the construction of the Cao'e River Railway Bridge. As for the extension of the Longhai Railway, the plan has also been decided, with the initial extension from Xi'an to Lanzhou. The Railway Department also plans to build the Su (Suzhou) Jia (Jiaxing) Railway as one of its new railway construction projects.

Sending Letters to Fujian and Guangdong Rice Merchants to Discuss Solutions
